
SET DEFINE OFF;
/


-- takto umožníme nastavování sloupců typu date a number
ALTER SESSION SET NLS_DATE_FORMAT = 'YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS';
ALTER SESSION SET NLS_NUMERIC_CHARACTERS = '. ';
/
-- 1: tabulky;
-- 2: triggery a pohledy;
-- 3: závislé objekty (lokalizace);
-- 4: číselníky;

DECLARE
  trans_id NUMBER(20, 0);
BEGIN
  ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
  UPDATE ee_transactions SET commit_id = enif_commitid_seq.nextval, commit_ts = systimestamp
  WHERE id = trans_id;
END;
/

commit;

SET DEFINE OFF;
/


-- takto umožníme nastavování sloupců typu date a number
ALTER SESSION SET NLS_DATE_FORMAT = 'YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS';
ALTER SESSION SET NLS_NUMERIC_CHARACTERS = '. ';
/

-- 2: triggery a pohledy;

-- 4: číselníky;

DECLARE
  trans_id NUMBER(20, 0);
BEGIN
  ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
  UPDATE ee_transactions SET commit_id = enif_commitid_seq.nextval, commit_ts = systimestamp
  WHERE id = trans_id;
END;
/

commit;

SET DEFINE OFF;
/

ALTER SESSION SET NLS_NUMERIC_CHARACTERS = '. ';

-- 2: triggery a pohledy;

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "EDA_DEAL_U"
BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON "EDA_DEAL"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
	trans_id number;
BEGIN
	ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
	:new.EE_TRANS_ID := trans_id;
	INSERT INTO "EDA_DEAL_C" t1(EE_CHANGE_ID, "EE_ITEM_ID", EE_CHANGE_TYPE, EE_TRANS_ID, t1."ACCEPTEDAT", t1."ACCEPTEDBYFK", t1."AGREEMENTBTSCAPFK", t1."AGREEMENTCAPACITYFK", t1."AGREEMENTFK", t1."AGREEMENTSTORAGEFK", t1."BALANCEZONEFK", t1."BOOKFK", t1."BUYACCOUNTFK", t1."COMMODITYETRADEFK", t1."CONFCOMPLETEFK", t1."COPARTYFK", t1."COPARTYIDONMARKETFK", t1."COPARTYTRADERFK", t1."CREATEDAT", t1."CREATEDBYFK", t1."CURRENCYETRADEFK", t1."DEALACCTYPEFK", t1."DEALDIRECTIONFK", t1."DEALID", t1."DEALINTERNALID01", t1."DEALKINDFK", t1."DEALMARKETCHARGESELECTFK", t1."DEALPURPOSEFK", t1."DEALSTATEFK", t1."DEALSTATEWANTEDFK", t1."DEALTYPEFK", t1."DELIVERYFROM", t1."DELIVERYTO", t1."DESCRIPTION", t1."ENTRYGRIDPOINTFK", t1."EXCHANGERATEACCFK", t1."EXCHANGERATEACCVFK", t1."EXCHANGERATEFK", t1."EXCHANGERATEVFK", t1."EXITGRIDPOINTFK", t1."EXTERNALID", t1."EXTERNALSHIPPERFK", t1."GPGGRIDFK", t1."GRIDETRADEFK", t1."GRIDLINEFK", t1."GRIDPOINTEXTERNALFK", t1."GRIDPOINTGROUPFK", t1."GRIDPOINTINTERNALFK", t1."INTERNALSHIPPERFK", t1."INVOICECONTRACTFK", t1."ISUNITEDDEAL", t1."MARKETFK", t1."MARKETMUIDFK", t1."MARKETUNITFK", t1."NAME", t1."PARENTFK", t1."PAYMENT", t1."PAYMENTACC", t1."PAYMENTAGG", t1."PRICE", t1."PRICEACC", t1."PRICEAGG", t1."PRICEMARGIN", t1."PRICEPAYMENTCURVEFK", t1."PRODUCTFK", t1."REASONTYPEFK", t1."RESETTIMESTAMP", t1."SALEACCOUNTFK", t1."SETTLEDAT", t1."SETTLEDBYFK", t1."SLEEVE", t1."TARGET_AGREEMENTCAPACITYFK", t1."TARGET_AGREEMENTCAPBTSFK", t1."TARGET_AGREEMENTSTORAGEFK", t1."TARGET_BOOKFK", t1."TARGET_MARKETFK", t1."TOTALFEEPAYMENTAGG", t1."VOLUME", t1."VOLUMECURVEFK", t1."VOLUMEHOURLYAVG", t1."SYS_VER")
	VALUES ("EDA_DEAL_S".nextval, :new."ID", 'u', trans_id, :new."ACCEPTEDAT", :new."ACCEPTEDBYFK", :new."AGREEMENTBTSCAPFK", :new."AGREEMENTCAPACITYFK", :new."AGREEMENTFK", :new."AGREEMENTSTORAGEFK", :new."BALANCEZONEFK", :new."BOOKFK", :new."BUYACCOUNTFK", :new."COMMODITYETRADEFK", :new."CONFCOMPLETEFK", :new."COPARTYFK", :new."COPARTYIDONMARKETFK", :new."COPARTYTRADERFK", :new."CREATEDAT", :new."CREATEDBYFK", :new."CURRENCYETRADEFK", :new."DEALACCTYPEFK", :new."DEALDIRECTIONFK", :new."DEALID", :new."DEALINTERNALID01", :new."DEALKINDFK", :new."DEALMARKETCHARGESELECTFK", :new."DEALPURPOSEFK", :new."DEALSTATEFK", :new."DEALSTATEWANTEDFK", :new."DEALTYPEFK", :new."DELIVERYFROM", :new."DELIVERYTO", :new."DESCRIPTION", :new."ENTRYGRIDPOINTFK", :new."EXCHANGERATEACCFK", :new."EXCHANGERATEACCVFK", :new."EXCHANGERATEFK", :new."EXCHANGERATEVFK", :new."EXITGRIDPOINTFK", :new."EXTERNALID", :new."EXTERNALSHIPPERFK", :new."GPGGRIDFK", :new."GRIDETRADEFK", :new."GRIDLINEFK", :new."GRIDPOINTEXTERNALFK", :new."GRIDPOINTGROUPFK", :new."GRIDPOINTINTERNALFK", :new."INTERNALSHIPPERFK", :new."INVOICECONTRACTFK", :new."ISUNITEDDEAL", :new."MARKETFK", :new."MARKETMUIDFK", :new."MARKETUNITFK", :new."NAME", :new."PARENTFK", :new."PAYMENT", :new."PAYMENTACC", :new."PAYMENTAGG", :new."PRICE", :new."PRICEACC", :new."PRICEAGG", :new."PRICEMARGIN", :new."PRICEPAYMENTCURVEFK", :new."PRODUCTFK", :new."REASONTYPEFK", :new."RESETTIMESTAMP", :new."SALEACCOUNTFK", :new."SETTLEDAT", :new."SETTLEDBYFK", :new."SLEEVE", :new."TARGET_AGREEMENTCAPACITYFK", :new."TARGET_AGREEMENTCAPBTSFK", :new."TARGET_AGREEMENTSTORAGEFK", :new."TARGET_BOOKFK", :new."TARGET_MARKETFK", :new."TOTALFEEPAYMENTAGG", :new."VOLUME", :new."VOLUMECURVEFK", :new."VOLUMEHOURLYAVG", :new."SYS_VER");

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "EDA_DEAL_D"
BEFORE DELETE ON "EDA_DEAL"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
	trans_id number;
BEGIN
	ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
	INSERT INTO "EDA_DEAL_C"(EE_CHANGE_ID, "EE_ITEM_ID", EE_CHANGE_TYPE, EE_TRANS_ID)
	VALUES ("EDA_DEAL_S".nextval, :old."ID", 'd', trans_id);
END;
/
						
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW "EDA_DEAL_H" AS
SELECT t1."EE_ITEM_ID" "ID", t1.EE_TRANS_ID EE_TRANS_ID, t1."ACCEPTEDAT", t1."ACCEPTEDBYFK", t1."AGREEMENTBTSCAPFK", t1."AGREEMENTCAPACITYFK", t1."AGREEMENTFK", t1."AGREEMENTSTORAGEFK", t1."BALANCEZONEFK", t1."BOOKFK", t1."BUYACCOUNTFK", t1."COMMODITYETRADEFK", t1."CONFCOMPLETEFK", t1."COPARTYFK", t1."COPARTYIDONMARKETFK", t1."COPARTYTRADERFK", t1."CREATEDAT", t1."CREATEDBYFK", t1."CURRENCYETRADEFK", t1."DEALACCTYPEFK", t1."DEALDIRECTIONFK", t1."DEALID", t1."DEALINTERNALID01", t1."DEALKINDFK", t1."DEALMARKETCHARGESELECTFK", t1."DEALPURPOSEFK", t1."DEALSTATEFK", t1."DEALSTATEWANTEDFK", t1."DEALTYPEFK", t1."DELIVERYFROM", t1."DELIVERYTO", t1."DESCRIPTION", t1."ENTRYGRIDPOINTFK", t1."EXCHANGERATEACCFK", t1."EXCHANGERATEACCVFK", t1."EXCHANGERATEFK", t1."EXCHANGERATEVFK", t1."EXITGRIDPOINTFK", t1."EXTERNALID", t1."EXTERNALSHIPPERFK", t1."GPGGRIDFK", t1."GRIDETRADEFK", t1."GRIDLINEFK", t1."GRIDPOINTEXTERNALFK", t1."GRIDPOINTGROUPFK", t1."GRIDPOINTINTERNALFK", t1."INTERNALSHIPPERFK", t1."INVOICECONTRACTFK", t1."ISUNITEDDEAL", t1."MARKETFK", t1."MARKETMUIDFK", t1."MARKETUNITFK", t1."NAME", t1."PARENTFK", t1."PAYMENT", t1."PAYMENTACC", t1."PAYMENTAGG", t1."PRICE", t1."PRICEACC", t1."PRICEAGG", t1."PRICEMARGIN", t1."PRICEPAYMENTCURVEFK", t1."PRODUCTFK", t1."REASONTYPEFK", t1."RESETTIMESTAMP", t1."SALEACCOUNTFK", t1."SETTLEDAT", t1."SETTLEDBYFK", t1."SLEEVE", t1."TARGET_AGREEMENTCAPACITYFK", t1."TARGET_AGREEMENTCAPBTSFK", t1."TARGET_AGREEMENTSTORAGEFK", t1."TARGET_BOOKFK", t1."TARGET_MARKETFK", t1."TOTALFEEPAYMENTAGG", t1."VOLUME", t1."VOLUMECURVEFK", t1."VOLUMEHOURLYAVG", t1."SYS_VER"
FROM
"EDA_DEAL_C" t1,
(SELECT EE_ITEM_ID, MAX(EE_CHANGE_ID) KEEP (DENSE_RANK FIRST ORDER BY COMMIT_ID desc, EE_CHANGE_ID desc) trans_change_id
  FROM "EDA_DEAL_C" ti INNER JOIN ee_visible_transactions v ON EE_TRANS_ID = v.id
  GROUP BY EE_ITEM_ID) g
WHERE t1.EE_ITEM_ID=g.EE_ITEM_ID and t1.EE_CHANGE_ID=g.trans_change_id and t1.EE_CHANGE_TYPE <> 'd';
/

	END IF;
END;

	trans_id number;

	:new.EE_TRANS_ID := trans_id;
	INSERT INTO "EDA_EXCHANGERATESERIE_C" t1(EE_CHANGE_ID, "EE_ITEM_ID", EE_CHANGE_TYPE, EE_TRANS_ID, t1."ACTIVE", t1."BASECURRENCYFK", t1."CAPTION", t1."COUNTERCURRENCYFK", t1."DESCRIPTION", t1."EXCHANGERATEFIXTYPEFK", t1."EXCHANGERATEPROVIDERFK", t1."KEY", t1."SAMPLEFK", t1."TIMEZONEFK", t1."TYPEFK", t1."SYS_VER")
	VALUES ("EDA_EXCHANGERATESERIE_S".nextval, :new."ID", 'u', trans_id, :new."ACTIVE", :new."BASECURRENCYFK", :new."CAPTION", :new."COUNTERCURRENCYFK", :new."DESCRIPTION", :new."EXCHANGERATEFIXTYPEFK", :new."EXCHANGERATEPROVIDERFK", :new."KEY", :new."SAMPLEFK", :new."TIMEZONEFK", :new."TYPEFK", :new."SYS_VER");

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW "EDA_EXCHANGERATESERIE_H" AS
SELECT t1."EE_ITEM_ID" "ID", t1.EE_TRANS_ID EE_TRANS_ID, t1."ACTIVE", t1."BASECURRENCYFK", t1."CAPTION", t1."COUNTERCURRENCYFK", t1."DESCRIPTION", t1."EXCHANGERATEFIXTYPEFK", t1."EXCHANGERATEPROVIDERFK", t1."KEY", t1."SAMPLEFK", t1."TIMEZONEFK", t1."TYPEFK", t1."SYS_VER"
FROM
"EDA_EXCHANGERATESERIE_C" t1,
(SELECT EE_ITEM_ID, MAX(EE_CHANGE_ID) KEEP (DENSE_RANK FIRST ORDER BY COMMIT_ID desc, EE_CHANGE_ID desc) trans_change_id
  FROM "EDA_EXCHANGERATESERIE_C" ti INNER JOIN ee_visible_transactions v ON EE_TRANS_ID = v.id
  GROUP BY EE_ITEM_ID) g
WHERE t1.EE_ITEM_ID=g.EE_ITEM_ID and t1.EE_CHANGE_ID=g.trans_change_id and t1.EE_CHANGE_TYPE <> 'd';
/

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER "EDA_NOMINATIONITEM_D"
BEFORE DELETE ON "EDA_NOMINATIONITEM"
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE
	trans_id number;
BEGIN
	ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
	INSERT INTO "EDA_NOMINATIONITEM_C"(EE_CHANGE_ID, "EE_ITEM_ID", EE_CHANGE_TYPE, EE_TRANS_ID)
	VALUES ("EDA_NOMINATIONITEM_S".nextval, :old."ID", 'd', trans_id);
END;
/
						
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW "EDA_NOMINATIONITEM_H" AS
SELECT t1."EE_ITEM_ID" "ID", t1.EE_TRANS_ID EE_TRANS_ID, t1."ACKVERSION", t1."ALLGREEN", t1."ANOVERSION", t1."CNFVERSION", t1."COMMAGGFK", t1."DELIVERYDATE", t1."ETRM", t1."ETRMHOURLYAVG", t1."IOTYPEFK", t1."NOMAGGPOWERFK", t1."NOMINT", t1."NOMINTBEFOREMATCH", t1."NOMINTGREYTEXT", t1."NOMINTRES", t1."NOMINTRESBEFOREMATCH", t1."NOMINTRESGREYTEXT", t1."NOMINTRESTIMEOUT", t1."NOMINTRESYELLOW", t1."NOMINTYELLOW", t1."NOMRES", t1."NOMRESBEFOREMATCH", t1."NOMRESGREYTEXT", t1."NOMRESPROVE", t1."NOMRESPROVEGREY", t1."NOMRESPROVERED", t1."NOMRESPROVEYELLOW", t1."NOMRESYELLOW", t1."SCHVERSION", t1."STATEFK", t1."VERSION", t1."SYS_VER"
FROM
"EDA_NOMINATIONITEM_C" t1,
(SELECT EE_ITEM_ID, MAX(EE_CHANGE_ID) KEEP (DENSE_RANK FIRST ORDER BY COMMIT_ID desc, EE_CHANGE_ID desc) trans_change_id
  FROM "EDA_NOMINATIONITEM_C" ti INNER JOIN ee_visible_transactions v ON EE_TRANS_ID = v.id
  GROUP BY EE_ITEM_ID) g
WHERE t1.EE_ITEM_ID=g.EE_ITEM_ID and t1.EE_CHANGE_ID=g.trans_change_id and t1.EE_CHANGE_TYPE <> 'd';
/

DECLARE
  trans_id NUMBER(20, 0);
BEGIN
  ee_get_transaction_id(trans_id);
  UPDATE ee_transactions SET commit_id = enif_commitid_seq.nextval, commit_ts = systimestamp
  WHERE id = trans_id;
END;
/

commit;
